Page 9

Important News

Japanese Finances After the September 18th Incident (Continued)

Tokyo Correspondence, Huai Ren

The large-scale issuance of public bonds is indeed a crux that the current Japanese finances cannot avoid. Although it is said that making up for financial deficiencies is not limited to the issuance of public bonds, under the joint cabinet of the military, they are extremely unwilling to implement tax increase policies that will have an immediate reaction. As a result, they cannot help but go down the path of debt. Indeed, the people of Japan are currently unable to endure further tax increases. For the sake of showing consideration for the people, the government is implementing the upper strategy of raising debts to ease social sentiment. However, this is also an unbelievable contradiction. How can people who cannot endure tax increases subscribe to such a huge amount of public bonds? According to the Minister of Finance, most of these public bonds will be subscribed by the Bank of Japan. At first glance, it seems that the issuance of public bonds no longer has any direct relationship with the people. However, the reality is not that simple.

As a result of most of the public bonds being borne by the Bank of Japan, currency will inevitably be issued in increased amounts for the Manchurian Incident expenses, deficit compensation, and unemployment projects. Needless to say, this will cause a currency inflation effect. The small portion of public bonds that are not borne by the Bank of Japan will generally be subscribed by the Deposit Bureau of the Ministry of Finance. Although the Deposit Bureau's subscription does not actively inflate the currency, in fact, when the Deposit Bureau bears the public bonds, it will inevitably issue its dead savings for turnover, which may actually passively promote currency inflation.

As a result of currency inflation, the price of currency will tend to plummet, and the relative price of goods will gradually tend to rise. According to the principles of the business cycle, it will inevitably be able to arouse temporary industrial investment. However, in today's era of lurking global economic crisis, this is easier said than done. Therefore, the recent result of Japan's currency inflation and rising prices not only cannot arouse the heat of industry, but will make the real wages of workers increasingly lower, and the property of those living on interest, small shopkeepers, and farmers will be invisibly and secretly requisitioned, eventually causing the middle class to rapidly fall into the proletariat, forming a clear struggle between the propertied and the propertyless, and building a new situation for Japan's future.

Since the September 18th Incident, a year has passed suddenly. Whether Japan can long-term and safely occupy my three northeastern provinces and carry out the annexation of Manchuria and Mongolia in name and reality depends entirely on the extent of our country's efforts in the future and the attitude of international opinion. However, the financial cracks that Japan has suffered as a result of September 18th and the terror in the future have already been placed before our eyes. This may give us a little comfort after extreme sorrow. However, it is absolutely not allowed for us to be optimistic because of this. (End)

The East Railway Eight Stations Issue that Triggered the Deterioration Between Japan and Russia

Russian Consul Lodges Strong Protest to the Puppet Diplomatic Office Shenyang Correspondence: The recent deterioration of relations between Japan and Russia was triggered by the Jiangyun Office of Puppet Harbin taking over the Jiangbin Wharf of the East Railway Eight Stations. At present, its negotiation industry has stopped. At the beginning of the incident, the Russian consul in Harbin had protested and sent it to the Puppet Harbin Diplomatic Office. Although this matter has been going on for many days, since it has caused a serious escalation of relations between Japan and Russia, it is not without a look at its value. The text is as follows: "This Consul General urges your Special Envoy to pay attention to the fact that the Northeast Jiangfang Fleet Headquarters is interfering irresponsibly and illegally with the Harbin Commercial Office Wharf Transportation Office of the Chinese Eastern Railway. This is destroying the Chinese Eastern Railway and the economic organization of the Soviet Union, and causing the eight stations soybeans to be unable to load and unload for a long time, causing significant losses. At the same time, regarding the illegal behavior of the headquarters, the Deputy Director Li Shaogeng and Deputy Chairman Kuzneitsov have jointly urged the Administrative Officer of the Special District, Zhang Jinghui, to pay attention. When meeting with this Consul General, they promised that the Manchurian government would take appropriate measures to avoid infringing on the rights of the Chinese Eastern Railway. However, the Northeast Jiangfang Fleet Headquarters and the Chinese Eastern Railway Commercial Office are interfering illegally with the affairs of the Commercial Office under the pretext of not renewing the contract, and engaging in irresponsible behavior, such as prohibiting the transportation affairs of the Commercial Office, detaining the wharf staff of the agency, or even detaining the wharf director, and destroying the keys, etc. According to the records of the wharf takeover and the general principles of the actions of the staff of the Northeast Jiangfang Fleet Headquarters, the above facts have been proven, and the rights and interests of the Chinese Eastern Railway have been significantly damaged. This is a serious protest to the Manchurian government. The Manchurian government must bear full responsibility for the damage caused to the economic organization of the Chinese Eastern Railway and the Soviet Union. This Consul General hopes that your Special Envoy will quickly stop the Northeast Jiangfang Fleet Headquarters from interfering with the wharf office of the Chinese Eastern Railway, fully restore the wharf rights, and take action against the Northeast Jiangfang Fleet staff's future insults and coercion against the Harbin Commercial Office staff, and within the scope of possibility, quickly request your government to respond quickly. Moreover, the Commercial Office has always stated verbally or in writing that it hopes to renew the contract. Especially according to the past and present contracts, the Northeast Jiangfang Fleet Headquarters has no right to the transportation affairs of the Commercial Office and the wharf (the property of the Chinese Eastern Railway). Soviet Consul General to Harbin, Slavutsky."

Corruption of Japanese Personnel in the Northeast

Two Japanese Advisors Guilty of Corruption and Illegal Activities

Opinions Differ Among Various Departments and Agencies

Politics Entirely Controlled by the Military

Even Law-Abiding Japanese People are Concerned

Suifenhe Correspondence: Japanese people often boast that they are united from top to bottom and consistent with the outside world. What the reporter has heard and witnessed here has proved that their statement is inaccurate. Although the Japanese ambition to annex the Northeast is fierce, it is actually divided into two factions: the rapid progress faction and the gradual progress faction. Even in terms of the Japanese people in the Northeast, those belonging to the Honjo Shigeru system of the Kwantung Army and the wandering people who have lived in the Northeast for many years belong to the rapid progress faction. Those belonging to the consulates and the Manchu Railway and cultural organizations advocate truly supporting the independence of the puppet country and Japan avoiding the name and residing in reality, secretly planning or manipulating it. This faction is the gradual progress faction, and the two factions are fighting fiercely in secret. However, because the military holds power, the current situation in the Northeast is completely controlled by the rapid progress faction. The gradual progress faction has retreated to a passive position due to the failure of its proposals. Therefore, in the puppet agencies, advisors, and consultants in various places in the Northeast, no Japanese gentleman has ever participated. Many Japanese people who have lived in Harbin and Heihe for many years and have always had a reputation have buried themselves in their original work and do not dare to climb high. There are actually quite a few people of this kind. A certain scholar once told the reporter that the current approach in Manchukuo is very bad, which only provokes the antipathy of the Chinese people. As a result, seeking speed is not achieved, and there is also fear of debt. There are more and more unemployed people in various places, production is declining, and food for the people this year is worrying, and security next year will be even more difficult to maintain. This kind of strategy is misled by ordinary soldiers. We have lived here for a long time and have not benefited from it. I am afraid that we will soon be affected by the economic downturn and may even go bankrupt and become unemployed. His words are quite representative of the opinions of some Japanese people here. It is a pity that the Japanese warlords are rampant and unscrupulous and do not know that the psychology of their own people is contrary to them. After the Kwantung Army of Japan took control of the life of the three northeastern provinces, wandering people from all over rose up to engage in activities, and even peddlers and pawns became consultants to the puppet state agencies. They forgot their original faces when they ascended to the sky in one step and were greedy and perverted the law without any scruples. For example, Horii, the advisor of the Harbour Ship Administration Bureau in Harbin, made a fortune of more than 100,000 in less than three months in office. The source of this wealth was the permission to build commercial ships. There has always been a surplus of Songhua River ships. The previous Shipping Administration Bureau had a limit of five ships to be built per year, but now Horii has lifted the ban. Anyone who has a movement to this end can build ships. As a result, more than a dozen commercial ships have been added to the Songhua River this year. Recently, the incident occurred and was captured by the Kwantung Army and will be punished. This is one example. The Puppet East Railway Guard Army Headquarters hired an advisor named Imai. This person was a retired soldier in his hometown. His original position was only a sergeant (i.e., subaltern). After being appointed as an advisor, he wore a lieutenant colonel's uniform and swaggered in the city, openly soliciting bribes and selling vacancies. He also had an opium addiction and would lie on a couch in the Chinese opium den every day. After he had enjoyed himself, he would brush off his clothes and leave without paying a penny. Recently, his special agency reported it to the military, and he was dismissed and investigated. A man named Ono was sent to take over. Imai occupied the official residence and refused to leave, and he was still guarded by four soldiers of the Guard Army when he went in and out. Ono was also a wandering man. Seeing that Imai was still claiming to be an advisor, he led four or five Koreans and went to look for him with whips. After they met, the two told each other about their dispatch. Their words were not in agreement, and they even fought each other. After all, Ono had more people, and Imai was whipped many times and staggered away. After going out, he still pointed his finger and scolded loudly, saying that he would not be able to report his grievances. This is another matter. From these two incidents, it can be seen that the Japanese occupation of the Northeast has never had a unified plan of organization. However, a group of wandering people and warlords stare wide-eyed every day, clench their fists, and act like tigers to the Chinese people. The Chinese people are subdued by their lewd power and submit their heads and listen to others. Again, in terms of the Japanese agencies in northern Manchuria, the opinions of the special agency, the military police, and the consulates are very different. Often, the military police are unaware of the affairs handled by the special agency and still interfere with them. The consulates are unaware of the affairs handled by the military police and handle them directly. The same is true for each division. The opinions between each individual are also deep. If puppet officials belong to the A agency system, the B agency must think of a way to restrict them. If they belong to the C and D agencies, the A and B agencies think of a way to remove them. Therefore, people say that the Japanese are consistent with the outside world, but it is not seen. What they can achieve, according to the reporter's observation, is only to despise the Chinese people and have no good feelings. Everyone thinks of the matter of slavery. (21st)

The Recovery of Qianjiang by the Suppression Army

Bandits Occupy Qianjiang for Seven Days and Loot More Than 100,000 Worth of Property

Liu and Huang Brigades Recover the County Seat and Kill Countless Bandits

The Kong Bandits, Numbering More Than 10,000, Plan to Capture Puchi

Hankou Correspondence: In recent months, the red bandits in Hubei Province have been struggling even harder due to the efforts of the army to suppress them. At the same time, in order to cut off communication and facilitate long-term resistance against the officers and soldiers, they have been actively communicating with various routes and forming mutual flanks. On the one hand, they are destroying transportation, so that the officers and soldiers cannot move quickly. The He section in central Hubei and western Hubei, the Kuang Xu section in eastern Hubei and northern Hubei, and the Kong Shen section in southern Hubei have all been launched simultaneously. The Yuan Duan is responsible for communicating with the Xiang River, the Kuang Bandits are responsible for destroying the Pinghan Road and the central Yangtze River, and the Kong Bandits are responsible for destroying the Xiang-E Road. Fortunately, General Commander Chiang is stationed in Hankou, the number of bandit suppression troops has increased, and the mobilization has been rapid, so the bandits' plans have not succeeded and they have suffered heavy losses. According to investigations, the He Duan bandits originally had the pseudo 7th, 8th, 9th, and 3rd divisions, together with the pseudo special agents and replenishment departments, totaling about four divisions, using Qianjiang, Tianmen, Jingshan, and Mianyang as their nests. Last month, the 10th Army troops joined forces with the Sichuan Army, Wang Lingji, and Fan Shaozeng, two divisions, to launch a general attack, and successively recovered Zaoshi and Qianjiang, killing countless bandits. It was not long before Qianjiang was lost again and Zaoshi was besieged again. On the 15th of this month, the armies launched a second general attack. Xu Yuanquan, Zhang Zhenhan, Xiao Zhichu, Wan Yaohuang, Liu Peixu, and others were all directing on the front line. On the 22nd, Xiao's division defeated the bandits attacking Zaoshi. On the 24th, Zhang's division and Liu Peixu's brigade captured Qianjiang County. At the same time, important bandit nests such as Diaochahu and Zhangjiegang were all cleared. Currently, He Chengjun and Xu Yuanquan are supervising the suppression of the remnants of the bandits on one side and rushing to handle local relief work on the other. As for the course of the battle, Xu, Zhang, and Xiao all sent telegrams to Hankou to report. Xu's telegram stated: "My Liu Peixu and Huang Xin brigades launched a general attack on Qianjiang on the morning of the 24th. After six hours of bloody hand-to-hand combat and more than a dozen charges, the city was completely recovered at noon, killing countless bandits and capturing prisoners everywhere. In addition to ordering active local relief work, we are also sending teams to follow up and pursue in order to completely clear the area." Zhang's telegram stated: "At dawn on the 24th, Huang Xin's brigade attacked Qianjiang. It was reported that they occupied the area at noon on the same day. The bandits fled towards X溝, and our cavalry is still pursuing." Xiao's telegram stated: "On the morning of the 22nd, our army launched an attack from Tianmen on the pseudo 7th and 8th divisions of the bandits who attacked my Zaoshi. At the same time, Yu Zhaolong's brigade also dispatched troops to attack. Seeing the large army suppressing them, the bandits fled west in a panic. My 10th brigade took the opportunity to pursue them, killing many bandits and capturing more than 20 guns. The bandits planned to retreat to the Qianjiachang and Wamiaoji areas. My army has followed up and suppressed them in the Qipomiao, Wuyanling, Wamiaoji, Tailimiao, and Yangjiachang battles, capturing a large number of bandits, machine guns, mortars, automatic rifles, carbines, and pistols, and mules and horses were seized. We also obtained the seal of the pseudo 9th division. Earlier, the He bandits' pseudo 7th and 9th divisions besieged Jingshan. My Xu group fought alone for 14 days and nights, and the bandits could not succeed. Later, in Qipomiao and Wuyanling, we inflicted heavy damage on the pseudo 7th division. We crushed the pseudo 8th division in Wamiaoji and Tailimiao, and again destroyed the pseudo 9th division, which had fled back from Qianjiang, in Yangjiachang. Countless people drowned. Duan bandits fled west in a panic. On the 20th, we pursued the bandits to Zhangjiegang. Hearing that the He bandits led the remnants of the pseudo 7th division to Zaoshi, we turned back to aid them. On the 22nd, we arrived in Zaoshi, and the bandits fled west again. In this battle, which lasted eight days, we chased for more than 300 li, and fought more than ten battles of various sizes, killing a large number of bandits and capturing more than 300 people alive, capturing more than ten machine guns, mortars, automatic rifles, and light machine guns, more than 300 carbines and pistols, more than 200 mules and horses, the seal of the pseudo 9th division, and dozens of flags, and destroying more than a dozen pseudo county governments." It is also heard that Qianjiang was lost for the second time on the early morning of the 18th of this month. About 5,000 He bandits entered the city, carrying out arson and looting, killing people like hemp, looting more than 100,000 yuan of property, and kidnapping more than 500 old and young men and women before retreating. Although they were released near Shayang, many died on the road, and the disaster was repeated, which is also pitiful.

In southern Hubei, the Kong bandits, led by He Chong, disturbed Guanbuqiao on the Wu-Chang Road on the 15th, and traffic was cut off for four days. On the 19th, it was restored to its original state. According to a recent telegram from Huang Yulin, the county magistrate of Puchi, to the Provincial Government and the Civil Affairs Department, the text said: "The red bandits who disturbed Guanbuqiao on the Wu-Chang Road are from the Kong He Chong Department, with about 10,000 people and more than 2,000 guns. It is rumored that the 85th Division stationed in Tongshan was robbed of more than 200 guns, and the 82nd Division stationed in Guanbuqiao was also robbed of 400 rifles, 4 machine guns, and 2 mortars. I don't know if this is true. The garrison in this county, in addition to telegraphically ordering Xie's battalion stationed in Tingsiqiao to rush to Xianning, also transferred Wu's battalion stationed in Shiqikeng and Long's battalion stationed in the county seat to reinforce the front. The bandits fled when they heard the news. My Xie's and Wu's battalions returned to their original defenses. It is now heard that more than 10,000 bandits with 400-500 guns have recently been discovered in Shushigang and Maishi in Tongcheng County, led by Shen Bandit Guozhen, who are currently in a stalemate with the Tongcheng Corps. According to recent confirmed reports, the National Army has recently obtained secret documents from the red bandits, whose plan is to break through Puchi and connect with the bandits north of the Yangtze River. Now the Kong and Shen bandits are very much imitating Puchi's example. The county magistrate has already consulted with the garrison to block the passes. Tingsiqiao and Shiqikeng Ferry have completed extremely strong defensive fortifications. All the corps in this county are divided into defenses in Longkeng, Xiaobai, Xindian, Chebu, and Wanguchang, supervising the brave teams and allocating defenses." (July 26th)

The Fujian Pacification Headquarters Controls the Various Troops Stationed in Fujian

Cai Tingkai Supervises Troops in Zhangzhou to Suppress Communists

Fuzhou Correspondence: Jiang Guangnai, the Director of the Fujian Pacification Headquarters, has requested sick leave, which has been approved by the Military Affairs Commission. Cai Tingkai, the Commander of the 19th Route Army, will act on his behalf. Because Cai himself is commanding the suppression of communists in Zhangzhou, he has appointed Deng Shizeng, the Chief of Staff of the Pacification Headquarters, to act on his behalf in all matters. A secretariat will not be established. The candidates for the directors of the Military Law and Military Ordnance Offices have not yet been determined. They were also ordered to submit reports detailing the names and numbers of officers and soldiers, the amount of military equipment and supplies, and the locations where the troops were stationed. He requested that immediate measures be taken to stop them. On the 22nd, the Pacification Headquarters telegraphed Yong'an, ordering Lu Xingbang to cease the attack pending investigation and resolution. It is unknown whether Lu's troops will comply. Regarding the suppression of bandits in western Fujian, after Cai Tingkai arrived in Zhangzhou from Xiamen, he ordered Zhang Zhen's 49th Division to advance from Nan'jing towards Longyan, Shen Guanghan's 61st Division to advance from Zhangzhou towards Nan'jing, and Qu Shounian's 78th Division to advance from Haicheng towards Zhangzhou. It was decided that Zhang's and Shen's divisions would take the front lines, and Qu's division would secure the rear. The plan is to first recover Longyan, then plan to attack the communist bandits' stronghold in Tingzhou on the Fujian-Jiangxi border. Currently, Zhang's division has advanced to Shizhong in Longyan, and Shen's division has advanced to Hexi in Nan'jing, close to the bandit lines. A major battle is expected to occur soon. (22nd)

Resolution of the Labor Strike at the Zhongxing Coal Mine in Zaozhuang

53 Trouble Makers Arrested

Jinan Correspondence: After the strike of external laborers at the Zhongxing Coal Mine in Zaozhuang, Han Fuju, the Chairman of the Shandong Provincial Government, sent Wang Jun, along with Gu Xianglin, the Chief of the Industry and Commerce Section of the Department of Industry, to Zaozhuang to investigate the cause of the strike and persuade the workers to resume work. After Wang and Gu arrived in Zaozhuang, they found thousands of workers gathered for a meeting. They gently advised them to resume work first, promising to find a solution to the profit-sharing problem. Most of the workers were willing to resume work, but trouble makers prevented them from doing so. Gu realized that communist elements were secretly instigating and inciting the workers. He then requested and received permission from the provincial government to send Kong Xiangsheng's regiment to suppress the unrest and prevent any unexpected events. Fifty-three trouble makers were arrested and imprisoned in the Yixian County government. A secret investigation is underway to identify and arrest the communist elements who initiated the labor strike and incited the workers, with the aim of imprisoning them. Regarding the resumption of work, Gu discussed and agreed with the company on a temporary solution: to issue bonuses. (Although the external laborers are contracted, the bonuses can be issued based on their performance, such as giving bonuses for exceeding the quota of coal mined, as an incentive. For example, if the original quota was 100 catties of coal per day for one yuan, if someone mines 110 catties in one day, which exceeds the quota by 10%, they will be given a bonus of 10 cents.) The company's bonus plan was also announced publicly. As a result, the workers gradually resumed work, and the labor strike has been resolved.

Minutes of the National Postal Joint Conference

Important Statement on the Puppet State Seizing Postal Rights

Urge Zhang and Tang to Implement Self-Defense and Recover Lost Territory

Mourn Martyred Postal Workers and Provide Relief to Their Families

The joint meeting of postal worker unions from across the country was held in Nanjing. Two sessions were held on the 26th, morning and afternoon. The details are as follows:

First Session: The first session began at 9:00 AM, with 51 representatives in attendance. Lu Jingshi chaired the meeting. The agenda included a proposal on how to respond to Japan's instigation of the puppet state's seizure of postal rights in the Northeast. Chen Zaiwen, the chairman of the proposal review committee, reported, based on proposals from the Bengbu and Kaifeng unions. The proposal reason was incorporated, and the following resolutions were made: (1) Request the government to resolutely implement a blockade of postal services in the Northeast. (2) Request the government to allow postal workers from the Northeast to enter the customs unconditionally and be assigned to serve in various post offices. (3) Suggest the Ministry of Communications telegraph the Universal Postal Union to jointly blockade Japanese postal services. (4) Issue a declaration explaining the reasons for blockading postal services in the Northeast and Japan. (Note) The discussion of this proposal was not concluded and will be moved to the next session. The meeting adjourned at 12:30 PM.

Second Session: The second session began at 2:00 PM, with 52 representatives in attendance. Shen Tiansheng chaired the meeting. After the meeting began, three minutes of silence were observed in mourning for the Shanghai anti-Japanese martyrs Pan Jiaji, Lu Chunhua, Chen Zude, and other workers who suffered due to the national crisis. The agenda included: (1) A proposal on how the union should respond to Japan's instigation of the puppet state's seizure of postal rights in the Northeast. The previous meeting did not complete the discussion, so it should be continued. The resolution was to continue the previous resolution, suggesting the Ministry of Communications to issue travel expenses to the Northeast employees entering the customs, according to the postal bureau's transfer regulations. However, postal assistants and lower-level postal workers should be issued an additional settlement allowance of 50 yuan per person, in addition to the travel expenses issued in accordance with the postal assistants transfer travel expenses. (2) Request the conference to telegraph Zhang Xueliang and Tang Yulin in Beiping and Rehe to immediately send troops to implement self-defense resistance and quickly recover lost territory. Request the government to declare a grand plan for resisting invasion and also petition the government. The resolution was passed. (3) Request the conference to telegraph national party, government, and military leaders to abandon personal prejudices and abolish internal strife to resist invasion and save the nation from danger. The resolution was passed. (4) Telegraph condolences to postal workers in the Northeast. The resolution was passed. (5) Request the conference to telegraph the national public to unite sincerely and jointly face the national crisis. The resolution was passed. (6) Telegraph to encourage postal workers across the country to strive to develop postal services. The resolution was passed. (7) Send a telegram to the Postal Economic System Research Committee, urging them to quickly research and implement methods to consolidate the postal foundation and submit a plan to the government. The resolution was passed. (8) Lu Chunhua, Chen Zude, Pan Jiaji, and other members of the Shanghai Postal Workers Union were brutally murdered by the enemy for participating in the anti-Japanese national salvation effort. Request the conference to mourn them and generously provide relief to their families to

Page 10

console their heroic souls and commend their loyalty. Resolutions: 1. The conference will observe three minutes of silence in mourning for the three martyrs, to be held on the spot. 2. Hold a memorial service (the name to be decided by the chairman's team), with the Nanjing and Shanghai unions responsible for preparation. 3. After the meeting, representatives from Shanghai will comfort the families of the three martyrs. 4. Postal workers unions from across the country will jointly build a martyrs' cemetery. 5. Regarding relief, 1. Investigate the family circumstances of the three martyrs and petition the National Government in the name of the conference for generous relief. 2. Postal workers unions from across the country will freely donate funds to provide relief to the families of the three martyrs, with the conference organizing committee having full authority to handle the matter. (9) Thoroughly improve the vacation system and implement a bonus system for not taking leave. The resolution was passed in principle and referred back to review.

Taicang

Budget Shortfall Leads to Change from Bureau to Section: This county has suffered consecutive years of famine, with barren land and impoverished people, causing the agricultural sector to face difficulties and all endeavors to be abandoned. Although the budget of each agency has been reduced repeatedly, it is still difficult to make ends meet. Recently, a portion of the land tax in the war zone has been ordered to be exempted, further reducing local revenue. Government expenditure should be further tightened to supplement resources. Gu Zhonghan, the head of the First District, Qian Jinpan, the head of the Second District, and Huang Baolin, the head of the Fourth District, specifically submitted a proposal to the first county administrative meeting of the 21st, recommending that the county's Education, Finance, Public Security, and Construction Bureaus be changed to specialized sections attached to the county government, to be handled by the county magistrate. The proposal has been approved and submitted to the province for approval and implementation.

Wuxi Prisoners Transferred to Taicang: The county prison and detention center in this county holds more than one hundred male and female prisoners who have been sentenced or are awaiting trial. In March of this year, all of them escaped, and none have been captured since. Recently, due to the hot weather and overcrowding in the Wuxi County Prison, inmates have been dying from infectious diseases daily. Chen Chuande, the county magistrate of Wuxi, considering this, specifically sent a letter to the county government of this county to discuss transferring a portion of the prisoners to Taicang to avoid the spread of infection. He has already sent officers to escort forty prisoners to Taicang, where they were received by prison officer Xia Xueqin for verification.

Kunshan

Bandits Extort Doctor: Wang Weibai, a doctor residing on South Street, received a threatening letter from bandits a few days ago. The letter stated that they had been in Kunshan for more than ten days and were aware that the doctor was highly regarded by patients. Therefore, they would not make unreasonable demands, but requested a loan of 300 yuan to be placed near the electric pole at the door at 12:00 PM on the 25th, wrapped in red paper and marked with a straw sandal. They would send someone to collect it. If the authorities were notified, they would take appropriate measures. After receiving the letter, Wang reported it to the Public Security Bureau for investigation. Qin Jieren, the Director of the Bureau, dispatched patrol leader Wang Ronghe with two armed patrol officers to ambush the area. At 12:30 AM on the 26th, Xu Xiangqu, a native of the city and former head of the Songjiang Tinglin Public Security Sub-bureau, passed by the location with a flashlight and noticed the paper package. As he bent down to pick it up, he was apprehended by Wang and the patrol officers, taken to the bureau, and detained. At 7:00 PM, after an interrogation by Section Chief Xia, Xu denied any involvement in the incident. Section Chief Xia, based on the statement, suspected that the case involved extortion and ordered him to be remanded in custody. On the 27th, he was sent to the county government for trial. The incident has attracted much attention throughout the city. Wei Wenyuan, the chairman of the County Chamber of Commerce, and Min Caichen, a doctor specializing in trauma, explained to Director Qin that Xu's behavior and reputation were generally good. However, as the principal offender had not been apprehended, it was feared that Xu would have difficulty being released temporarily.

However, the school has been suspended for many days, and matters such as student enrollment and other proceedings for the next semester urgently need to be handled.

Danyang

Communist Criminal Escapes from Prison: Zhu Xilin, a communist criminal from Taixing, was sent by the Provincial Security Department to the Danyang Detention Center for temporary detention. Yesterday at 11:00 AM, Zhu suddenly escaped from the prison by climbing over the wall. By the time the prison guards realized it, he had disappeared without a trace. Yu Xinbo, the guard on duty, also fled for fear of punishment. Prison guards are now searching everywhere for him. The guard has been arrested in Zhenjiang. Whether there is a suspicion of releasing the prisoner is currently under investigation.

Epidemic Outbreak in Urban and Rural Areas: The weather has been extremely hot in recent days, and an epidemic is raging in the city. More than one hundred people have died one after another. The county government, the Public Security Bureau, and the Relief Institute are preparing to establish a summer epidemic prevention center and have considerable equipment for preventive measures. It is now reported that a cholera epidemic has occurred in Baziqiao and Muqiao in the 12th district of the northern countryside. More than 30 people have died in a few days. For prevention purposes, the people in the township are required to bury the dead on the same day without allowing them to hold funerals and stay to prevent the spread of the epidemic.

Zhenjiang

Meeting of Executive Committee of the Zhenjiang Chamber of Commerce: The Zhenjiang Chamber of Commerce held its 25th Executive Committee meeting yesterday, chaired by Yu Xiaochuan. The resolutions included: (1) Appointing Wu Tixian as the custodian of the National Defense Fund for the Prohibition of Imported Goods. (2) Restricting the establishment of new foreign goods stores to concentrate capital and talent. A draft plan will be submitted to the general membership meeting for discussion. (3) Ratifying the membership of Xiangxin Qu Powder Company and Changshengtai. The Chamber of Commerce will convene a joint meeting of various industry associations at 3:00 PM today to discuss the procedures for nominating Chamber of Commerce member representatives by each industry association.

Planning a Large-Scale Domestic Goods Market: Lu Xiaobo, Yu Xiaochuan, Wu Tixian, Zhou Zigeng, Yang Guangyu, Hu Xiwu, Huang Bofu, Liu Zhuyun, and others in this port, considering that the provincial capital is flooded with foreign goods and lacks a proper domestic goods market, plan to raise funds to survey locations and build a large-scale domestic goods market. This is currently in progress.

The Beijing-Tangshan Road has been Completed: The realignment project of the Beijing-Hangzhou Highway's Beijing-Tangshan section was originally scheduled for completion by the end of June. However, due to rainfall on 31 days in April, May, and June, work could not be carried out and had to be extended to early August. However, the Jiangsu Construction Department considered the project extremely important and could not be delayed any further. It strictly ordered Director Yu of the Engineering Office to supervise the contractors to rush the construction day and night. According to a telegram report from Director Yu of the Engineering Office to the department, the various projects in the Beijing-Tangshan section have been completed successively. The contractors completed the work a few days or more than ten days ahead of schedule, in accordance with the contract's provisions for extending the completion date due to rainy days.

Yangzhou

Autumn Harvest in a Drought: This year's summer has been especially dry, with the scorching sun shining for more than twenty days without a drop of rain. As a result, the crops in the Jiangbei area are withering badly. If it does not rain again, not only will the mountain

fields be hopeless, but even the polder fields will yield nothing.

Shareholder Turmoil at Yutong Company: At the previous shareholders' meeting of Yutong Salt Company on Zuowei Street, Yangzhou, after the election of new directors, shareholder Fang claimed that the consolidation of shares and the sudden influx of new shareholders supporting the election of new directors was unfair. He hired lawyer Huang Qi to apply to the county court for mediation and declare the election invalid. The court hearing was on the 24th, but the opposing party, Chen Xiangchen, did not appear. Lawyer Huang requested that the mediation be declared invalid so that a formal lawsuit could be filed. In addition, Fang has learned that the company's capital has suffered losses, with debts exceeding four times the capital. He has separately submitted reports to the Ministry of Finance, the Ministry of Industry, the Salt Affairs Administration, and the Huaiyun Administration, requesting that they order an increase in capital or declare liquidation to avoid affecting commercial finance and damaging shareholders' rights. Once approval is obtained, a special shareholders' meeting will be convened to discuss the matter.

Cholera Epidemic and Drought Leading to Famine: The cholera epidemic in Jiangdu has been detailed in previous reports and is even more severe in the past two days. On the 24th, 26 people in this city died from the epidemic, mostly poor young adults. From early morning to noon on the 25th, five people had died in one corner of the old city. Agricultural products are suffering from drought. If it does not rain again in ten days, the Xishan area will face famine again.

Nantong

Change of County Court President: Cai Yang, the president of the Nantong County Court, returned to his ancestral home in Hunan due to the death of his father. Long Shiliang, a judge, was temporarily appointed to act as president. Cai also firmly resigned to the High Court, which has been approved. Chen Xianwen has been separately appointed to come to Tong to take over.

Joint Defense Zone Investigating Bandits and Communists: Due to the unrest of bandits and communists in Tong, Ru, Hai, and Taiqi, the joint defense zone is arresting escaped bandits and communists. In Yidong District, more than 160 people are on the wanted list. Among them, those who have been mistakenly implicated have submitted applications to the district headquarters for exoneration. The district director has convened a meeting to publicly resolve the change in handling. Those who are wanted are required to report to the

district security corps for investigation within two weeks. If they have been implicated, they are allowed to be released on bail. If they fail to come within the deadline, they will still be strictly pursued.

Gaoyou

County Magistrate Allocates Emergency Military Certificates: The county government received a joint order from the Department of Finance and Construction yesterday, stating that the provincial government has decided to issue 600,000 yuan in Emergency Military Certificates to the entire province of Jiangsu to fund urgent construction projects. The amount allocated to Gaoyou has been reviewed and approved at 6,210 yuan, which should be promptly prepared and reported. The Jiangbei Canal Project Aftermath Committee has sent Commissioner Liu to the post to deliver the certificates to the county government. It is heard that County Magistrate Li will convene a meeting of various agencies and district chiefs to discuss the allocation method.

Haimen

Epidemic Spreads, Many Deaths: In recent days, the epidemic has been spreading in Haimen County, with several deaths occurring daily. Yang Shao'an, a reporter for the Dagong Daily, also died from the epidemic the day before yesterday. The newspaper has temporarily ceased publication because of this. Yesterday (the 25th), another eleven people died in the county, and the city statistics show that seventy to eighty people have died in the past ten days. Businesses throughout the county and the city have widely hung white paper flags, praying for rain. Many townships have banned slaughtering and selling fish, meat, shrimp, and crabs. If it does not rain again, not only will cotton, beans, and corn wither and die, but the epidemic may spread further.

Jiaxing

Meeting on Rice Loans in the First District: The Rice Loan Branch of the Poor Peasants in the First District of Jiaxing was established a few days ago by the district chief Mei Shoren convening a meeting of the township and town heads. Mei Shoren, Zhu Lisān, and Mei Jinjiang were nominated as standing committee members. It was also resolved that (1) the poor peasants will be reported by the township and town heads in conjunction with the neighborhood chiefs, to be completed within one week; (2) the rice loans will be processed completely within two weeks; (3) the quantity of rice loaned will be prescribed as follows: (A) regardless of the number of mouths, those with three or fewer people will borrow two dou and five sheng; (B) those with five

or fewer people will borrow five dou; (C) those with ten or fewer people will borrow one dan.

Investigating and Prohibiting Gambling at Nanhu: Nanhu Lake in Jiaxing is a scenic spot in Hezhong. During the summer season, painted boats gather like clouds. However, singing, choosing beauties, and gambling have always been strictly prohibited. This year is different. The sound of mahjong and singing continues day and night, and the water and land police do not interfere. Yesterday, the County Executive Committee resolved to send a letter to the water and land police to strictly investigate and prohibit gambling at Nanhu.

Ningbo

Director of the Civil Affairs Department to Inspect Ningbo: Lu Bichou, the director of the Civil Affairs Department of Zhejiang Province, set off from the province a few days ago to inspect various places in Wenzhou and Taizhou. Yesterday, the political and police agencies in Ningbo received a telegram from Wenzhou, stating that Director Lu is scheduled to come to Ningbo on the Pingyang ship from Yuhuan today (the 27th) to inspect the government affairs of Yin County and the cadres of the security corps.

Joint Military and Police Investigation Office Established: Wang Haonan, the garrison commander of Ningbo, in order to maintain local security and rectify military discipline, jointly organized a Joint Military and Police Investigation Office with the 6th Regiment of the Ningbo Security Team and the Ningbo Public Security Bureau, and appointed Xu Zhixia as the director of the office. The director was sworn in at the Tianhou Temple yesterday and formally established the office.

Fuyang

Accident Involving Qianjiang and Dahua Ships: On the 22nd, the Qianjiang and Dahua Shipping Companies' Jiangkai passenger ships departed from Tong. The Hengxing ship of the Qianjiang Company arrived in Fu before long and was about to set off, but because there were many tugboats, it could not go straight. As it was heading downstream, it was about to turn its head when the Dahua ship was about to enter the

port. The two ships could not give way in time, and the Qianjiang Company's Hengxing ship collided with the tugboat of the Dahua ship. The tugboat was smashed, and hundreds of boxes of tea and several passengers on board fell into the water. Fortunately, people nearby tried their best to rescue them. One passenger was rescued with serious injuries. After the Public Security Bureau's Water Police Team learned of the incident, they took the accountants and sailors of the two ships to the bureau for interrogation.

Shengxian

Kidnapping Case Occurs at Qingfeng Ridge: Qingfeng Ridge is a necessary route for people from Sheng and Xin to Ningbo, Hangzhou, and Shaoxing. The mountains are towering, and there are no villages in the vicinity. Yesterday (the 22nd) at around 10:00 AM, several shipping boats

were traveling upstream on the Shanxi River, including a pointed-head boat hired exclusively by Sheng and Xin passengers. Because the boat was inspected by the security corps for a long time when it reached Sanjie, it fell behind. Unexpectedly, when it reached the vicinity of the Qingfeng Temple, more than a dozen bandits suddenly appeared, standing on the shore, all wearing firearms. They shouted for the boat to approach the shore, boarded the boat all at once, and ransacked boxes and cabinets, robbing all the cash and valuables of the passengers. They also kidnapped five men and one woman, releasing one man and one woman each on the shore. The names of the four kidnapped people are unknown. It is heard that one of them is an accountant from a certain cloth shop in the city.

Bandits Burn Down Zhang Zuojun's Residence: On June 15, several bandit letters were found in Waizhai Village, Baini Dun Township, First District, Sheng County, and sent to the village head for distribution. One of the letters was delivered to Zhang Zuojun's house, extorting 6,000 yuan. It was stipulated that the land be accepted. If he did not comply, he would be killed and the house burned down without mercy. The letter was signed by Zhang Guosheng, the Commander of the Hongjun Army. Subsequently, bandits came in person to urge him several times, but Zhang ignored them. The bandits held a grudge and came to the village on the afternoon of the 21st of this month to burn the house. In an instant, the fire blazed into the sky, and the multi-story house and the bungalows were turned to ashes. Then, they wanted to burn the residence of Zhang Qingshan, Zhang Zuojun's brother, but were spared after the neighbors pleaded. The bandits left a letter (this letter was delivered to Zhang Zuojun, Zhang Qingshan, and Zhang Nansan, stating that they must leave within three days) and fired shots to intimidate them before leaving.

Anqing

Hu's 1st Regiment Triumphantly Arrives in Anhui　The 1st Regiment of Hu Zongnan's 1st Division, under orders to suppress bandits in Anhui, has repeatedly achieved success. The bandit atmosphere in Anhui has been slightly reduced. This regiment, the 1st Regiment of the 1st Brigade of the said division, arrived in Anhui on the afternoon of the 23rd via the Shu County land route and is stationed in various locations. When the division first entered Anhui, in addition to the original troops, it also commanded the Independent 33rd Brigade under Tang Yunshan. Recently, Chairman Jiang of the Military Affairs Commission sent a telegram ordering the 1st and 2nd Anhui Garrison Brigades under Shi Zhongcheng and Li Yanqing to be placed under the control and dispatch of the division. Division Commander Hu Zongnan will soon come to the province from Shucheng to discuss everything with Chairman Wu Zhongxin and inspect Li Yanqing's brigade, which has recently arrived in the province. According to military sources, the division has received orders to open the Han River waterway, and ships have docked in Anhui awaiting transport, but this has not yet been confirmed.

The Longdai River Case Has Been Resolved　The Anhui Construction Department previously sent engineer Li Jixiang to Su County to join engineers Lei Hongji from the Huai River Guidance Committee and commissioners from Jiangsu Province to investigate the dispute over the Longdai River between Su and Xiao counties. The Construction Department now reports that the dispute has been temporarily resolved, with Xiao County agreeing to fill a section of both the Longdai and Xiao rivers, totaling more than three li in length. Workers from Su County have also been withdrawn. It is proposed that after surveying the Suyi River downstream, then along the Longdai River to the upper reaches of Xiao County, they will return to Beijing to discuss a fundamental plan.

Educational News Highlights

The Resignation of the Director of Higher Education Has Not Been Approved

Nanjing, 27th　Guo Xinsong, Director of the Department of Higher Education of the Ministry of Education, has not had his resignation approved and has been granted another ten days of leave.

President Li Siguang of Central University Has Arrived in Beijing

Nanjing, 27th　Li Siguang, President of Central University and Vice Chairman of the Reorganization Committee, arrived in Beijing on the 26th.

The Ministry of Education Will Not Participate in the International Congress of Mathematicians

Nanjing, 27th　The Ministry of Education plans not to send representatives to the International Congress of Mathematicians to be held in Zurich, Switzerland, from September 4th to 12th.

The Ministry of Education's First Phase of Administrative Plan

| Three Months of the 21st Year (July, August, September)

The Ministry of Education has submitted its planned administrative plan for the first three months of the 21st year (July to September) to the Executive Yuan for the record. The original plan is as follows:

Regarding Higher Education Matters

(1) Convene a meeting of presidents of national colleges and universities; (2) Formulate measures for the conclusion and aftermath of the National Labor University; (3) Handle the screening and testing of graduates and students of unregistered and closed private colleges and universities; (4) Send personnel to inspect private colleges and universities that are in the process of registration; (5) Formulate measures to remedy losses suffered by public and private colleges and universities due to the Shenyang and Shanghai incidents; (6) Formulate austerity measures for national colleges and universities during the national crisis; (7) Send personnel to Europe to study education.

Regarding Secondary Education Matters

(1) Promulgate middle school regulations; (2) Promulgate curriculum standards for junior high schools and senior high school general courses; (3) Draft a budget format for secondary schools; (4) Stipulate standards for the allocation of operating expenses for secondary schools; (5) Convene a committee to compile standards for moral education in secondary schools; (6) Draft standards for secondary school equipment.

Regarding Elementary Education Matters

(1) Promulgate elementary school regulations; (2) Promulgate curriculum standards for elementary schools and kindergartens; (3) Draft kindergarten regulations; (4) Organize a committee to draft standards for the compilation of elementary school textbooks; (5) Review elementary school textbooks and children's books; (6) Draft propaganda measures for elementary education.

Regarding Overseas Chinese Education Matters

(1) Reorganize the Overseas Chinese Education Design Committee; (2) Handle the registration of Overseas Chinese schools.

Regarding Social Education Matters

(1) Issue an overview of social education for the 18th year; (2) Compile and print questionnaires from provinces and cities regarding people's schools and vocational supplementary schools for reference by provinces and cities; (3) Continue to investigate the implementation of social education in provinces and cities; (4) Continue to organize historical materials on social education administration; (5) Convene a national sports conference; (6) Prepare for the establishment of the Central Education Museum; (7) Print and distribute statistical tables of the national social education overview for the 20th year; (8) Print and distribute a directory of national libraries; (9) Investigate world-renowned libraries and collect library catalogs; (10) Petition the Executive Yuan to organize a Central Antiquities Preservation Committee in accordance with the organizational regulations of the Central Antiquities Preservation Committee; (11) Print and distribute the national calendar for the 22nd year.

Regarding Mongolian and Tibetan Education Matters

(1) Continue to select and translate Mongolian and Tibetan textbooks and Party doctrine books; (2) Translated Mongolian and Tibetan textbooks urgently need to be printed and distributed to various Mongolian and Tibetan regions for use; it is proposed to urge the Ministry of Finance to promptly allocate 10,000 yuan from the Mongolian and Tibetan education funds for the 20th year for printing; (3) Actively investigate the status of education in various Mongolian and Tibetan regions in the 19th year in order to compile it into the national education yearbook for the 19th year; (4) The Mongolian and Tibetan Class of Central University has been suspended due to funding issues; it is necessary to continue to plan for funding and reopen it in the next semester.

Enrollment at Central University Is Still Difficult to Be Optimistic

Constrained by National Issues

The Misfortune of Middle School Graduates

Since Central University was reorganized under President Li Siguang, who arrived in Beijing this Monday, all issues concerning professors and students have been resolved. However, the middle schools that had suspended enrollment requested the Central University Reorganization Committee to consider the prospects of the graduates of various schools so that they would have a place to continue their education. Chairman Cai Yuanpei has been in Shanghai for many days, and other committee members here, due to the repeated requests of representatives from various middle schools, also went to Shanghai but found no satisfactory solution. The Reorganization Committee, together with the education administrative authorities, resolved the reorganization plan. After the plan was executed by the Executive Yuan and the Ministry of Education by order, there were practical difficulties. Only if those implementing education and executing orders consider that there is room for consideration or delay the execution can a solution be sought. The Reorganization Committee has no possibility of automatically reconsidering the matter or proposing another suggestion. If various middle schools are indeed in difficult circumstances, they can directly study the matter with the President of Central University in the future. According to those familiar with the situation of all parties, enrollment at Central University may be difficult to achieve. As the education administrative authorities are now determined to rectify the situation, the merger of Shanghai University and the University Council and the temporary suspension of enrollment at Peking University are inevitable. How can a concession be made for the enrollment of Central University alone, which would affect the original position regarding other schools? For example, Central University teachers have not resolved the issue of salary arrears, even though they advocate paying full salaries for February, March, April, May, June, and July, because the government cannot make a special case for one school. Therefore, there is still no solution. (Central University has not yet paid 50% of July's salary.) This is because it is constrained by national issues.

Zhejiang University Secretariat Organization Expanded

New Dean of the College of Engineering Takes Office

Enthusiastic Registration of New Students in Shanghai

National Zhejiang University, including the Colleges of Liberal Arts and Sciences, Engineering, and Agriculture, has had its administrative structure divided among the three colleges due to historical reasons. Although there is a Secretariat, it only handles routine documents. Recently, President Cheng Tianfang, feeling that the measures were scattered and ineffective, decided to centralize administrative power in the Secretariat. In the future, the deans of each college will focus on teaching and academic equipment. The Secretariat will be divided into six sections: Documents, Registration, Accounting, Affairs, Graphics, and Publications, each with a director, and the Secretary-General will be in charge of all sections. Huang Huabiao, an education expert and former Director of the Guangxi Education Department, has been hired as Secretary-General and will also serve as Director of the Documents Section. Yu Ziyi, the secretary, will also serve as Director of the Registration Section, Ouyang Xianyi, the secretary, will also serve as Director of the Graphics Section, Meng Guangzhao will be the Director of the Affairs Section, Tang Zimei will be the Director of the Accounting Section, and Hu Changqi will be the Director of the Publications Section. The internal organization of the Secretariat has been largely completed and is currently busy taking over the administrative part of each college. Xue Shaoqing, the newly hired dean of the College of Engineering, arrived in Hangzhou yesterday and has taken over the affairs of the college. Xue received a degree in electrical engineering from Cornell University in the United States. After returning to China, he served as the head of the Department of Electrical Engineering at Central University for four years and was recently hired as a specialist member of the Construction Committee. He is rich in both knowledge and experience, and the faculty and students of the college warmly welcomed him upon his arrival. The school's first entrance examination for new students was held in Shanghai, and 800 applicants registered, which can be described as enthusiastic. The examination has now been completed, and the test papers have been sent to Hangzhou for review. The results will be announced in about a few days, and the second entrance examination will be held in Hangzhou around August 20th. In terms of moral education, the school will abolish the Moral Education Office and replace it with life instructors to guide students' lives on campus, starting from the next semester. Gan Jiaxin, Qiu Zuanzu, He Changrong, and Tang Liling have been hired to take on these positions.

Jiangyin Private Zhengcun Middle School Adds a Senior High School

Jiangyin Private Zhengcun Middle School was founded with funds donated by local merchants such as Qian Weiqi. It has been ten years since it was first named Zhengcun College, with junior high school and national studies departments. In the 17th year of the Republic of China, it was approved for registration and renamed Zhengcun Junior Middle School, with Ren Jicheng as the principal. It has held six junior high school graduations. Recently, the school felt that there were many junior high school graduates in the county, and the quota for local senior high school students was insufficient to meet the needs. The school board convened a meeting a few days ago, attended by school board members Zhu Tinghua, Wu Zengyuan, Xue Deyu, Zhang Chongzhi, Chen Gang, and others, totaling more than ten people. It was decided that starting from the 21st year, a senior high school would be added, recruiting one class of first-year students in the general studies department. Temporary and regular expenses have been arranged, and Ji Chengfan has been reappointed as the principal. It has been reported to the Education Department for approval to add the school in accordance with the current regulations for private schools.

Relief for Losses of Schools in the War Zone

Post-War Commission for the Songhu War Zone

A Meeting Will Be Held Once Song Arrives in Shanghai to Discuss the Matter

(Central News Agency) Since the January 28th Incident, the schools in the Songhu war zone have been devastated by artillery fire and trampled by the Japanese army. The losses are incalculable. The affected schools had previously jointly petitioned the Ministry of Education for relief. Minister Zhu presented the matter for discussion at the 52nd Executive Yuan meeting, and it was resolved that the Post-War Commission for the Songhu War Zone (yesterday's newspaper mistakenly wrote Post-War Commission for the Shanghai War Zone) should convene a meeting in the near future specifically to discuss the issue of relieving the losses of the schools in the Songhu War Zone, and report the discussion process and results. It is now known that the Post-War Commission for the Songhu War Zone will convene a committee meeting to discuss this issue after Chairman Song Ziwen arrives in Shanghai next time.

Jinan University Students' Movement to Protect the School

Yesterday's Reception for Journalists

Representatives Went to Beijing to Issue a Declaration

Cai Yuanpei Promised to Ask the Authorities to Withdraw Their Decision

Riri News reported that after the Executive Yuan passed the Ministry of Education's proposal to merge the Colleges of Law and Education of National Jinan University, the overseas Chinese students felt a great sense of responsibility. In order to safeguard their vital interests and the cause of overseas Chinese education, in addition to the faculty and the school protection association of all students successively sending representatives to Beijing to petition and issuing a school protection declaration, they specifically held a reception for reporters from local newspapers and news agencies at the Central Press Club at 3:00 p.m. yesterday to report all the details, which are recorded below:

The Process of the Merger　Since the outbreak of the January 28th Incident, all cultural institutions in Shanghai, such as the Commercial Press, the Oriental Library, and Tongji and Jinan Universities, were destroyed by artillery fire and suffered heavy losses. The Ministry of Education, due to financial difficulties, had difficulty restoring them in a short time. Also, because Shanghai and Beijing were close by, and the capital already had the establishment of the College of Law and the College of Education at Central University, the decision was made to merge the Colleges of Law and Education of Jinan University in order to save expenses and avoid duplication of academic systems and to transfer the students of the two colleges to Central University.

Reasons for Protecting the School　When the association hosted the reporters, Zhu Dunli and Ye Damou first reported the reasons for protecting the school, stating that the greatest mission of Jinan University lies in training overseas Chinese children and cultivating advanced academic knowledge to enable them to develop overseas, especially the Colleges of Education and Law, which have the task of cultivating overseas Chinese teachers and studying the political economy of Southeast Asia. Therefore, without Jinan University, there would be no overseas Chinese education. Without the Colleges of Education and Law, the overseas Chinese children returning to China would not receive teacher training and the opportunity to study Southeast Asian law and economics. If they were transferred to other schools, they would not only have an awkward situation due to the different lives and languages of overseas Chinese children, but would also fundamentally lose the original intention of cultivating overseas Chinese education. According to the facts, the College of Commerce of Central University was completely destroyed by artillery fire in the Shanghai war, but there was no news of contraction or merger. The College of Medicine of Central University has not been heard to have merged with Tongji University due to economic exhaustion. So why does the Ministry of Education only want to merge the Colleges of Law and Education of Jinan University, which has a special mission? Therefore, our school protection movement has full reasons and will never stop until our goal is achieved.

Cai Yuanpei's Statement　Mr. Cai Jiemin specially came to the Central Press Club at 3:00 p.m. yesterday. The society sent three representatives, Zhu Dunli, Tao Yi, and Tang Jingzong, to state the reasons for protecting the school. Mr. Wu immediately expressed his complete acceptance and promised to make strong suggestions to the government authorities in order to withdraw their decision.

Petition in Beijing　The school protection movement felt that the merger of the two colleges of law and education would have a significant impact on overseas Chinese education. A decision was made at the meeting the day before yesterday to send Hu Shouyu, Du Ping, and Zeng Yifu with petitions to the Executive Yuan and the Ministry of Education in Beijing the night before to request the withdrawal of the decision.

Visiting School Board Members　In addition to sending personnel to Beijing to petition, the association also specially sent representatives Zhu Dunli and others today to visit the two school board members, Wu Tiecheng and Kong Xiangxi, to state the reasons for protecting the school and request their strong support.

Graduates Go to Beijing to Petition

Nanjing, 27th　Wang Wei, representative of the Jinan University Alumni Association, and others, asked the Ministry of Education to withdraw the decision to merge the colleges. The Ministry of Education sent Secretary Gao to meet them, explaining the government's views on reorganizing the universities. Their request was not understood.

Current Graduates of Labor University Protect the School

The special commissioner sent by the Ministry of Education to take over the current graduates of Labor University was the subject of the recommendation of representatives Wang Fuhai and Wen Jimu. When the commissioner visited the school the day before yesterday, they expressed their opinions, asking the Ministry of Education to publish the Labor University's revival plan before taking over the school, and also questioned the problem of introducing the work of the current graduates. It was heard that yesterday morning, a general meeting of all graduate students staying at the temporary school site on Ladu Road was convened, with 24 people present, chaired by Zeng Xiyou, and the following resolutions were made: (1) Please ask the Ministry of Education to announce the school board of the school as soon as possible; (2) Send representatives to visit the receiving commissioner again; (3) Contact former graduates to organize a general association of graduates to discuss school protection matters; (4) Urge the Ministry of Education to introduce work and request temporary living expenses before being hired, and more than ten other items.

Farewell Reception for Students Going Abroad Will Start Preparing

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau and the Universal Chinese Students' Association initiated preparations for a farewell reception for this year's students going abroad. It was previously reported that the College of Commerce of National Central University, the Minbao Museum, the Chenbao Museum, and the Commercial Press had participated. Yesterday, Guanghua University, the Tsinghua Alumni Association, Qixiu Girls' Middle School, the Huamei Cooperative Society, the International Issues Research Association, the Great Evening News, and the Zhonghua Book Company agreed to participate. It is heard that the preparatory committee will hold a preparatory meeting at 5:00 p.m. next Monday at Hua'an Building on the eighth floor across from the Racecourse to discuss all the proceedings. Each group has appointed representatives to attend.

Boy Scout Council Moves Back to Original Address

Will Convene Citywide Service Personnel for Intensified Training

The Shanghai Boy Scout Council, formerly located at Yi Xiang Li 128, Ximen, was about to close down due to lack of funds after the January 28th Incident. Fortunately, the Moore Memorial Church on Sanma Road offered preferential treatment, so it moved to the headquarters of the Boy Scout group at the church to continue its work and handle war zone services. Now that Shanghai has returned to normal, it recently moved to 167 Wenmiao Road, Ximen, to work. It is recently known that the 24th Standing Committee Meeting of the Central Committee has passed the resolution to have the Civil Movement Guidance Office send a letter to the Ministry of Education to order the education halls and bureaus of all provinces and cities to order the education bureaus and schools of all counties under their jurisdiction to stop the training of volunteer soldiers. From now on, this training will be incorporated into Boy Scout training. In order to promote the Boy Scout cause, the council will convene citywide service personnel and intensify training to live up to the expectations of the Central Committee.

The Japan Tennis Club Wins the Championship by a Mere Two Points

|| Closing of the Lawn Tennis League ||

The China Tennis Club displayed its might yesterday, unexpectedly defeating the formidable Japan Tennis Club by a score of 10-5 at the Jiangwan Japan Tennis Court. The Group A Lawn Tennis League also concluded, with the China Club losing the championship to the Japan Club by a mere two points, marking the fourth consecutive year the Japan Club has retained the title, causing much sighing and stamping of feet.

Exceptional Results Against the Japan Club

(1) Lin Binhua and Zheng Zhaojia defeated Hyosuke Tawara and Machida 6-1, 8-6, 6-1

Losing the Title by Just Two Points is a Cause for Triple Regret

Before yesterday's final, the Japan Tennis Club led with a total score of 73 to 66 over the China Tennis Club. Out of yesterday's 15 matches, if China could win 12, they would win the championship. If they won 11, it would be a tie, requiring another final. Unexpectedly, they won exactly 10, resulting in a loss by two points. The excellent opportunity to win the championship slipped away, causing much dismay. The total scores of the two teams are as follows:

Runner-up, China Club, 105 matches, 76, 29

Yesterday's Championship Lost Despite Being Within Reach

Looking at the preceding results, the China Club controlled the entire court yesterday. Scores of 12-3 and 11-4 were entirely possible. However, the 10-5 result shows a championship lost despite being winnable. The first team of Lin and Zheng was unstoppable, winning the first set 6-1. They were leading 5-2 in the second set, but because they took victory too easily, the Japanese team caught up to 5-5 and ultimately they conceded the set 8-10. Isn't this strange? If the third and fifth teams could have each won one more set, everything would have been resolved. In the final set of the second team, they fought hard but lost 7-9. Wasn't this extreme bad luck? Overall, the Japanese team was actually quite ordinary and unremarkable.

Lin Binhua and Zheng Zhaojia Overcome Formidable Opponents

Yesterday's interest was focused on the first team of Lin and Zheng versus Tawara, as neither team had lost before. This was essentially a battle for the Shanghai doubles championship and a prediction of the Rotary Cup outcome.

Lin and Zheng Control the Entire Court In terms of both skill and strategy, Lin and Zheng were able to dominate and control the entire court, making a straight-set victory a foregone conclusion. Tawara served, but Lin and Zheng immediately won the point. The Japanese team then regained a game, but after that, Lin and Zheng went on a rampage, winning five consecutive games to win the first set.

Winning Too Easily Leads to Loss In the second set, Zheng served with undiminished momentum, holding a 3-0 lead firmly in their grasp. However, bad luck struck, and Lin and Zheng became complacent, gradually relaxing because they thought victory was too easy, and they still led 5-2. Unexpectedly, the Japanese team seized the opportunity and won three consecutive games. The Chinese team still led 6-5 and 7-6, but Zheng gradually showed signs of fatigue, and with a loss of serve, the second set was lost.

Lin Binhua's Masterpiece After losing that point in the second set, they redoubled their efforts in the third set, winning it easily 6-1. Lin Binhua's performance yesterday, facing such a formidable opponent, can be described as a rare masterpiece. His angled shots, placements, net play, and re-serves were all highly praised. On several occasions, his re-serves left Tawara unable to return the ball. Zheng Zhaojia still has a weakness in his forehand, often being in a passive position. The Japanese team's defeat was due to Machida's poor performance, but Machida has improved greatly compared to last year.
